# For specific combinations of culture, religion and other such triggers
# Will pick the first valid one it finds in list

#00 - COLONIAL GOVERNMENTS

#00a - Specific Cultures and Religions

iberian_colonial_government_title_1 = {
	rank = {
		1 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
		2 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
		3 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
		4 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
		5 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
		6 = CAPTAINCY_GENERAL
	}
	
	ruler_male = {
		1 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		2 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		3 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		4 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		5 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		6 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
	}
	
	ruler_female = {
		1 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		2 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		3 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		4 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		5 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
		6 = CAPTAIN_GENERAL
	}
	
	trigger = {
		government = republic
		culture_group = iberian
		colonial_gov_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = title_1
			has_country_flag = title_1
		}
	}
}

		6 = PATRIARCHATE

		6 = PATRIARCH

	}
}

		OR = {
			religion = chaldean
			religion = coptic
		}
		any_owned_province = { OR = { has_province_modifier = coptic_patriarchate has_province_modifier = chaldean_patriarchate } }
	}
}

south_andean_monarchy_title_1 = { #Aymara and Quechua
	rank = {
		1 = AYLLU
		2 = AYLLU
		3 = AYLLU
		4 = AYLLU
		5 = AYLLU
		6 = AYLLU
	}
	
	ruler_male = {
		1 = MALLKU #Head of a traditional community in the Andes
		2 = MALLKU
		3 = MALLKU
		4 = MALLKU #Head of State
		5 = MALLKU
		6 = MALLKU #Emperor
	}
	
	ruler_female = {
		1 = MALLKU #Head of a traditional community in the Andes
		2 = MALLKU
		3 = MALLKU
		4 = MALLKU #Head of State
		5 = MALLKU
		6 = MALLKU #Emperor
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			primary_culture = quechuan
			primary_culture = aimara
		}
		religion = inti
		government = monarchy
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = title_1
			has_country_flag = title_1
		}
	}
}
